# About this item
* PERSONAL SOUND: Flex&#39;s 12mm speaker technology delivers a personalized audio experience, adapting to your preferences. Whether you're a bass enthusiast, a lover of crystal-clear highs, or somewhere in between, Flex delivers a tailored listening experience and ensures an immersive listening experience.
* SAFE LISTENING: Discover a fresh approach to open ear listening with Flex's ergonomic Clip-on cuff design, meticulously engineered to provide a secure yet lightweight fit. Designed for extended wear, offers superior sound without compromising safety. This stylish alternative to traditional earbuds allows you to enjoy music, podcasts, and calls while staying aware of your surroundings.
* EXTENDED BATTERY LIFE: Flex Open earbuds features 7+ hours of wireless playtime in each earbud and 14+ additional hours from the charging case. That’s 21+ total hours of Bluetooth 5 playtime.
* CONNECT TO MULTIPLE DEVICES: With Bluetooth Multipoint you enjoy the versatility of transitioning seamlessly from device to device. Hop from podcast on your computer to a call on your mobile. You can connect simultaneously to two devices –mobile, laptop and/or computer.
* JLAB APP: With the new JLab app, you’ll have control to customize the touch controls, and sound to your personal preference –or use the presets for JLab Signature, Balance or Bass Boost. Plus get software updates for your product right when they’re available. Available on the App or Google Play Store.
* BETTER BASS: Prepare to be blown away by Flex's astonishing bass performance, thanks to our bass boost algorithm you’ll enjoy booming sound at any level. Feel the rhythm and depth of your favorite tracks like never before, as Flex delivers a truly immersive audio experience.
* Everyday proof IPX4: You want an earbud that can keep up with you. The Flex Open Earbuds are everyday proof for your life on-the-go with an IPX4 rating. That's durability for all life’s adventures.
* Clear Calls; Whether you're in a busy office or a noisy city street, the Flex Open Earbuds noise-canceling mic ensures crystal clear calls. The MEMS mic in each bud helps eliminate background noise, ensuring that your voice is heard loud and clear on the other end.
* Google Fast Pair: Enjoy even more effortless pairing with an Android device with Google Fast Pair. When you take out your earbuds and have a supported Android device, you’ll see a pop-up enabling you to connect via Bluetooth. Don’t worry if you’re not an Android user, JLab earbuds will connect with any Bluetooth enabled device like iPhone with just a couple taps.
* INCLUDES: Flex Open Wireless Earvyds, Charging Case, 3 Sets Gel Tips: Small, Medium, Large, JLab Two Year Warranty.

## Product description
OPEN-EAR FREEDOM. EFFORTLESS FIT.
Introducing the Flex Open Earbuds, the perfect blend of technology and ergonomic design for your everyday life. The revolutionary clip-on cuff design ensures a secure, lightweight fit, seamlessly blending your surroundings with immersive open-ear sound. Whether you're running errands, walking, or navigating a busy city, these earbuds adapt to your personal sound preferences for an unparalleled listening experience. With seamless Bluetooth connectivity, you can effortlessly switch from a podcast on your laptop to a call on your phone, while noise-canceling microphones ensure crystal-clear calls. Built for your dynamic lifestyle, the Flex Open Earbuds are your ideal everyday companion.
PERSONAL SOUND
Flex's 12mm speaker technology delivers a personalized audio experience, adapting to your preferences. Whether you're a bass enthusiast, a lover of crystal-clear highs, or somewhere in between, Flex delivers a tailored listening experience and ensures an immersive listening experience.
SAFE LISTENING
Discover a fresh approach to open ear listening with Flex's ergonomic Clip-on cuff design, meticulously engineered to provide a secure yet lightweight fit. Designed for extended wear, offers superior sound without compromising safety. This stylish alternative to traditional earbuds allows you to enjoy music, podcasts, and calls while staying aware of your surroundings.
EXTENDED BATTERY LIFE
Flex Open earbuds features 7+ hours of wireless playtime in each earbud and 14+ additional hours from the charging case. That’s 21+ total hours of Bluetooth 5 playtime.
CONNECT TO MULTIPLE DEVICES
With Bluetooth Multipoint you enjoy the versatility of transitioning seamlessly from device to device. Hop from podcast on your computer to a call on your mobile. You can connect simultaneously to two devices –mobile, laptop and/or computer.
JLAB APP
With the new JLab app, you’ll have control to customize the touch controls, and sound to your personal preference –or use the presets for JLab Signature, Balance or Bass Boost. Plus get software updates for your product right when they’re available. Available on the App or Google Play Store.
BETTER BASS
Prepare to be blown away by Flex's astonishing bass performance, thanks to our bass boost algorithm you’ll enjoy booming sound at any level. Feel the rhythm and depth of your favorite tracks like never before, as Flex delivers a truly immersive audio experience.
Everyday proof IPX4
You want an earbud that can keep up with you. The Flex Open Earbuds are everyday proof for your life on-the-go with an IPX4 rating. That's durability for all life’s adventures.
Clear Calls
Whether you're in a busy office or a noisy city street, the Flex Open Earbuds noise-canceling mic ensures crystal clear calls. The MEMS mic in each bud helps eliminate background noise, ensuring that your voice is heard loud and clear on the other end.
Google Fast Pair
Enjoy even more effortless pairing with an Android device with Google Fast Pair. When you take out your earbuds and have a supported Android device, you’ll see a pop-up enabling you to connect via Bluetooth. Don’t worry if you’re not an Android user, JLab earbuds will connect with any Bluetooth enabled device like iPhone with just a couple taps.
INCLUDES
Flex Open Wireless Earvyds, Charging Case, 3 Sets Gel Tips: Small, Medium, Large, JLab Two Year Warranty.

These JLab Flex Open Earbuds are perfect for me as someone who can’t wear normal earbuds. They don’t fall out and they are comfortable. You can hear both songs and calls clearly, even in fairly loud outdoor areas. The teal colour adds a nice touch too. I highly recommend these earbuds.

Carlos Aguirre Hernández
##### *4.0 out of 5 stars*Buenos para el precio, formato de sujeción interesante y comodo.
Reviewed in Mexico on 22 September 2025
Colour: Black**Verified Purchase
Me llegó un verde agua en vez del negro. Comenzado por ahí, mal por el vendedor.
Segundo: Los quiero para el gimnasio nada más, y para correr en la caminadora, al mismo tiempo de poder escuchar mis alrededores, por lo cual funcionarán bien. Tienen el volumen suficiente para tapar la música del gimnasio, que también los quiero para eso.
Ahora, comparando con unos Shokz Open Run Pro 2 que uso para todo (correr y entrenar en exteriores, trabajar en oficina o en casa, tomar videollamadas, o sea todo menos escuchar música en silencio (para eso tengo unos Marshall Major 2 alambricos que se han comportado como unos campeones).
Dire lo siguiente:
No tiene bajos potentes, los Shokz los barren.
La calidad de construcción se siente barata, de nuevo, los Shokz los barren, y a simple vista se nota la diferencia de materiales.
Son muy cómodos, no los sientes en los oídos, igual que los Shokz, sin embargo, los Shokz tienen esa diadema que aporta seguridad, no se caerá por algún manotazos sin querer o así, pero la diadema de los Shokz puede ser incómoda en ciertos movimientos, empate.
La batería dura igual que los Shokz, pero los jlab tienen su case que los carga, punto para el jlab.
Los Shokz dejan pasar más sonido, aunque los jlab también, si vas a correr o hacer cosas en el exterior dónde puedas ser atropellado, son ligeramente más seguros los Shokz, pero los jlab también son muy buenos. Para eso prefiero los Shokz, pero si solo tuviera los jlab, harían la chamba muy bien.
Ambos tienen su app, que son igual de funcionales, punto para ambos.
Diciendo esto, los Shokz son 2.5 veces más caros (los Shokz los compré a 2500 pesos en oferta, el precio normal es 4500 pesos o sea 4.5 veces más caros que los jlab), así que relación precio, los jlab cumplen bien por el precio, nada que quejarme por eso, también los compré porque este formato tipo clip en los oídos jamás lo había usado, si son eficientes, compraré los Shokz Open dots One.
Ahora, ya falta ver su duración, los Shokz Open Run Pro 2 son un tanque, se me han caído, los uso como 8 horas al día diario, los cargo a cada rato, me han acompañado por viajes de trabajo a Sudamérica, los uso para videollamadas del trabajo, de celular, etc. Ya veremos cuanto duran estos Jlab que solo los usaré para el gimnasio y correr en caminadora, y cuando tenga que salir por algo en transporte público, llámese metro, (no uso autobús ni microbus en la CDMX, son tardado a e ineficientes, y los microbuseros son unos primates manejando).

*4.0 out of 5 stars*##### Buenos para el precio, formato de sujeción interesante y comodo.
Reviewed in Mexico on 22 September 2025
Me llegó un verde agua en vez del negro. Comenzado por ahí, mal por el vendedor.
Segundo: Los quiero para el gimnasio nada más, y para correr en la caminadora, al mismo tiempo de poder escuchar mis alrededores, por lo cual funcionarán bien. Tienen el volumen suficiente para tapar la música del gimnasio, que también los quiero para eso.
Ahora, comparando con unos Shokz Open Run Pro 2 que uso para todo (correr y entrenar en exteriores, trabajar en oficina o en casa, tomar videollamadas, o sea todo menos escuchar música en silencio (para eso tengo unos Marshall Major 2 alambricos que se han comportado como unos campeones).
Dire lo siguiente:
No tiene bajos potentes, los Shokz los barren.
La calidad de construcción se siente barata, de nuevo, los Shokz los barren, y a simple vista se nota la diferencia de materiales.
Son muy cómodos, no los sientes en los oídos, igual que los Shokz, sin embargo, los Shokz tienen esa diadema que aporta seguridad, no se caerá por algún manotazos sin querer o así, pero la diadema de los Shokz puede ser incómoda en ciertos movimientos, empate.
La batería dura igual que los Shokz, pero los jlab tienen su case que los carga, punto para el jlab.
Los Shokz dejan pasar más sonido, aunque los jlab también, si vas a correr o hacer cosas en el exterior dónde puedas ser atropellado, son ligeramente más seguros los Shokz, pero los jlab también son muy buenos. Para eso prefiero los Shokz, pero si solo tuviera los jlab, harían la chamba muy bien.
Ambos tienen su app, que son igual de funcionales, punto para ambos.
Diciendo esto, los Shokz son 2.5 veces más caros (los Shokz los compré a 2500 pesos en oferta, el precio normal es 4500 pesos o sea 4.5 veces más caros que los jlab), así que relación precio, los jlab cumplen bien por el precio, nada que quejarme por eso, también los compré porque este formato tipo clip en los oídos jamás lo había usado, si son eficientes, compraré los Shokz Open dots One.
Ahora, ya falta ver su duración, los Shokz Open Run Pro 2 son un tanque, se me han caído, los uso como 8 horas al día diario, los cargo a cada rato, me han acompañado por viajes de trabajo a Sudamérica, los uso para videollamadas del trabajo, de celular, etc. Ya veremos cuanto duran estos Jlab que solo los usaré para el gimnasio y correr en caminadora, y cuando tenga que salir por algo en transporte público, llámese metro, (no uso autobús ni microbus en la CDMX, son tardado a e ineficientes, y los microbuseros son unos primates manejando).

##### *5.0 out of 5 stars*Buy these, love them soooo much!
Reviewed in the United Kingdom on 18 June 2025
Colour: Teal**Verified Purchase
I have tried open ears before because I love the argument that, 1. They're not inside your ears, 2. Surround sound is not cut out and yet I can still here the music to an acceptable quality that I expect. I've tried 2 other open ears manufacturers, both Chinese manufacturers with British distributers, they did not last 6 months and of course being cheap tat from China, there's no guarantee or warranty!! These though, from JLab are a breath of fresh air, thankyou!
I find them very comfortable to wear. I jog and hill climb, therefore wear them for neigh on 2 hours, and there's times I think they have fallen out because I cannot honestly feel them. The quality from open ears is what I expect, it's clear and satisfactory. If I want pure sound, I'll hook myself up to a £10k music system, with either £5k speakers or £5k ear phones, fully enclosed like Mickey Mouse, listening to vinyl records played at either 33rpm or 45rpm! I do not understand why there's criticism about bass, they're open ears! Please be advised if this is a big issue to you, download an equaliser app, they have all the pre sets you want and for free.
I love these, they are so responsive, and when I'm in the mountains, jogging, this is what I need! Well done JLab.
Once used JLab
Why did you choose this product over others?:
I will not keep wasting my money on Chinese cheap, no name tat with British distributers! Jlab is a well known name in the ring of things.

Ivy
##### *5.0 out of 5 stars*Perfect for casual listening!
Reviewed in the United States on 25 July 2025
Colour: Black**Verified Purchase
So, for starters, I do a lot of gardening and spend plenty of time in my yard; these have yet to slip or fall out, even on the stickiest sweaty summer days.
They’re super comfortable and I absolutely love the design and fit. They fit just around the outside of your ears, like a cuff and the tiny speaker is just resting on your ear. I love that they don’t actually go into your ears (like an airpod would) and that they don’t fully cover your ears, like full size headphones do. Perfect for when you want to be aware of your surroundings while catching up on podcasts, audiobooks or just having some background music while working out or getting chores done.
They’re super lightweight, I’ve never felt like they were weighing me down or tugging.
The battery life is great, I actually haven’t charged them since I received them two weeks ago, and the battery sensor says they’re still full (shocking!)
The JLab app allows you to fully customize the levels of the audio, which is handy if you’re into that sort of thing. You can also totally customize the tap functions (pause, skip, volume up/down, google/siri) in the app as well, although I’ve opted to turn the majority of gestures off except for pause and volume controls.
They function well, and as expected. They’re not massively expensive, so I wouldn’t expect a full on studio experience from $30-40 earbuds, but the sound quality is great.
If you need earbuds that allow you to be aware of your surroundings, don’t slip, and don’t cost an arm and a leg, you’ve found them.
The only downside is finding a case cover, the charging port is on the back of the case, not the bottom, and the case is wider than it is tall, so it’s quite difficult to find a match. (I’ve opted to use a case intended for Bose Ultra Open earbuds, but the charging port isn’t in the right spot, so the cover needs to be removed once i finally get around to charging the case itself. Not a huge issue, but something to keep in mind if you want to have a secure and accessible case cover.)

# Product Summary: JLab Flex Open Earbuds, Teal, Clip-on Cuff Design, Wireless Open-Ear Audio Freedom Effortless Fit, Safe Listening, Bluetooth Multipoint, Customize with The JLab App
From JLab
4.1 out of 5 stars, 882 ratings
[Customer reviews](?ref=dp_product_quick_view#customer-reviews_feature_div)
## Price
No featured offers available
[Other sellers](?ref=dp_product_quick_view#dynamic-aod-ingress-box)
[Other sellers](?ref=dp_product_quick_view#unqualifiedBuyBox)
## About this Item
* PERSONAL SOUND: Flex's 12mm speaker technology delivers a personalized audio experience, adapting to your preferences. Whether you're a bass enthusiast, a lover of crystal-clear highs, or somewhere in between, Flex delivers a tailored listening experience and ensures an immersive listening experience.
* SAFE LISTENING: Discover a fresh approach to open ear listening with Flex's ergonomic Clip-on cuff design, meticulously engineered to provide a secure yet lightweight fit. Designed for extended wear, offers superior sound without compromising safety. This stylish alternative to traditional earbuds allows you to enjoy music, podcasts, and calls while staying aware of your surroundings.
* EXTENDED BATTERY LIFE: Flex Open earbuds features 7+ hours of wireless playtime in each earbud and 14+ additional hours from the charging case. That’s 21+ total hours of Bluetooth 5 playtime.
* CONNECT TO MULTIPLE DEVICES: With Bluetooth Multipoint you enjoy the versatility of transitioning seamlessly from device to device. Hop from podcast on your computer to a call on your mobile. You can connect simultaneously to two devices –mobile, laptop and/or computer.
* JLAB APP: With the new JLab app, you’ll have control to customize the touch controls, and sound to your personal preference –or use the presets for JLab Signature, Balance or Bass Boost. Plus get software updates for your product right when they’re available. Available on the App or Google Play Store.
* BETTER BASS: Prepare to be blown away by Flex's astonishing bass performance, thanks to our bass boost algorithm you’ll enjoy booming sound at any level. Feel the rhythm and depth of your favorite tracks like never before, as Flex delivers a truly immersive audio experience.
* Everyday proof IPX4: You want an earbud that can keep up with you. The Flex Open Earbuds are everyday proof for your life on-the-go with an IPX4 rating. That's durability for all life’s adventures.
* Clear Calls; Whether you're in a busy office or a noisy city street, the Flex Open Earbuds noise-canceling mic ensures crystal clear calls. The MEMS mic in each bud helps eliminate background noise, ensuring that your voice is heard loud and clear on the other end.
* Google Fast Pair: Enjoy even more effortless pairing with an Android device with Google Fast Pair. When you take out your earbuds and have a supported Android device, you’ll see a pop-up enabling you to connect via Bluetooth. Don’t worry if you’re not an Android user, JLab earbuds will connect with any Bluetooth enabled device like iPhone with just a couple taps.
* INCLUDES: Flex Open Wireless Earvyds, Charging Case, 3 Sets Gel Tips: Small, Medium, Large, JLab Two Year Warranty.
## Product description
OPEN-EAR FREEDOM. EFFORTLESS FIT. Introducing the Flex Open Earbuds, the perfect blend of technology and ergonomic design for your everyday life. The revolutionary clip-on cuff design ensures a secure, lightweight fit, seamlessly blending your surroundings with immersive open-ear sound. Whether you're running errands, walking, or navigating a busy city, these earbuds adapt to your personal sound preferences for an unparalleled listening experience. With seamless Bluetooth connectivity, you can effortlessly switch from a podcast on your laptop to a call on your phone, while noise-canceling microphones ensure crystal-clear calls. Built for your dynamic lifestyle, the Flex Open Earbuds are your ideal everyday companion.
PERSONAL SOUND Flex's 12mm speaker technology delivers a personalized audio experience, adapting to your preferences. Whether you're a bass enthusiast, a lover of crystal-clear highs, or somewhere in between, Flex delivers a tailored listening experience and ensures an immersive listening experience.
SAFE LISTENING Discover a fresh approach to open ear listening with Flex's ergonomic Clip-on cuff design, meticulously engineered to provide a secure yet lightweight fit. Designed for extended wear, offers superior sound without compromising safety. This stylish alternative to traditional earbuds allows you to enjoy music, podcasts, and calls while staying aware of your surroundings.
EXTENDED BATTERY LIFE Flex Open earbuds features 7+ hours of wireless playtime in each earbud and 14+ additional hours from the charging case. That’s 21+ total hours of Bluetooth 5 playtime.
CONNECT TO MULTIPLE DEVICES With Bluetooth Multipoint you enjoy the versatility of transitioning seamlessly from device to device. Hop from podcast on your computer to a call on your mobile. You can connect simultaneously to two devices –mobile, laptop and/or computer.
JLAB APP With the new JLab app, you’ll have control to customize the touch controls, and sound to your personal preference –or use the presets for JLab Signature, Balance or Bass Boost. Plus get software updates for your product right when they’re available. Available on the App or Google Play Store.
BETTER BASS Prepare to be blown away by Flex's astonishing bass performance, thanks to our bass boost algorithm you’ll enjoy booming sound at any level. Feel the rhythm and depth of your favorite tracks like never before, as Flex delivers a truly immersive audio experience.
Everyday proof IPX4 You want an earbud that can keep up with you. The Flex Open Earbuds are everyday proof for your life on-the-go with an IPX4 rating. That's durability for all life’s adventures.
Clear Calls Whether you're in a busy office or a noisy city street, the Flex Open Earbuds noise-canceling mic ensures crystal clear calls. The MEMS mic in each bud helps eliminate background noise, ensuring that your voice is heard loud and clear on the other end.
Google Fast Pair Enjoy even more effortless pairing with an Android device with Google Fast Pair. When you take out your earbuds and have a supported Android device, you’ll see a pop-up enabling you to connect via Bluetooth. Don’t worry if you’re not an Android user, JLab earbuds will connect with any Bluetooth enabled device like iPhone with just a couple taps.
INCLUDES Flex Open Wireless Earvyds, Charging Case, 3 Sets Gel Tips: Small, Medium, Large, JLab Two Year Warranty.
